	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php') != 'dab25553655e2e809ccad61b3c1375d1de352b65') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php') !== 'dab25553655e2e809ccad61b3c1375d1de352b65') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php') !== 'ed8e4cf46d069a3b57892f95cb36d72ff043522e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php') !== 'dab25553655e2e809ccad61b3c1375d1de352b65') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusAltId.class.php');
		}
	}
}
